<script type="text/javascript" data-script-priority="highest">
  (function() {
    const bindPageTransitions = () => {
      window.addEventListener('pagereveal', async (e) => {
        if (!e.viewTransition) {
          return;
        }

        const clickedNextArticle = !!localStorage.getItem('next-aritcle-clicked');
        localStorage.removeItem('next-aritcle-clicked');

        let transitionClass = 'none';

        // We are going from a page to another, and we used the next article click to do so
        if (e.viewTransition && clickedNextArticle) {
          transitionClass = 'push';
        }

        document.documentElement.dataset.transition = transitionClass;
        await e.viewTransition.finished;
        delete document.documentElement.dataset.transition;
      });
    };

    bindPageTransitions();
  })();
</script>

let _comscore = window._comscore || [];
let comscoreTriggered = false;

const checkGdpr = (tcData) => {
  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(tcData)) {
    if (value) return "1";
  }
  return "0";
};

const updateComscore = (gdpr) => {
  if (!comscoreTriggered) {
    console.log('[COMSCORE] Loading Comscore beacon with GDPR:', gdpr);
    _comscore.push({ c1: "2", c2: 10476312, cs_ucfr: gdpr });
    (function() {
      var s = document.createElement("script"), el = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0]; s.async = true;
      s.src="https://sb.scorecardresearch.com/cs/10476312/beacon.js";
      el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
    })();
    comscoreTriggered = true;
    console.log('[COMSCORE] Beacon script loaded successfully');
  }
};

const callback = (tcData, success) => {
  console.log('[COMSCORE] TCFAPI callback triggered:', { success, eventStatus: tcData?.eventStatus });

  if(success && tcData.eventStatus === 'tcloaded') {
    __tcfapi('removeEventListener', 2, (success) => {
      if(success) {
        const gdprValue = checkGdpr(tcData.purpose.consents);
        console.log('[COMSCORE] GDPR consents processed:', gdprValue);

        updateComscore(gdprValue);
      }
    }, tcData.listenerId);
  } else {
    console.log('[COMSCORE] TCFAPI not successful or not loaded, proceeding without GDPR data');
    updateComscore("");
  }
}

// Only load Comscore if user is not a logged-in ContentPass subscriber
const initializeComscore = () => {
  console.log('[COMSCORE] Initializing Comscore analytics...');
  
  if (typeof cp === 'function') {
    console.log('[COMSCORE] ContentPass function found, checking authentication...');
    
    cp('authenticate', (err, user) => {
      console.log('[COMSCORE] ContentPass authentication result:', { 
        error: err, 
        user: user, 
        hasValidSubscription: user?.hasValidSubscription?.() 
      });
      
      // Only load Comscore if there's an error OR user doesn't have a valid subscription
      if (err || !user || !user.hasValidSubscription()) {
        console.log('[COMSCORE] User not authenticated or no valid subscription - LOADING Comscore');
        if (window.__tcfapi) {
          __tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, callback);
        }
      } else {
        console.log('[COMSCORE] User has valid ContentPass subscription - SKIPPING Comscore');
      }
    });
  } else {
    console.log('[COMSCORE] ContentPass function not available - LOADING Comscore by default');

    // If cp function is not available, load Comscore by default
    if (window.__tcfapi) {
      __tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, callback);
    }
  }
};

// Initialize when DOM is ready
if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initializeComscore);
} else {
  initializeComscore();
}
